all_samples <- readRDS("/researchers/caitlin.page/cf_nano/r_output/all_rrbs_samples.rds")
optiles_all <- readRDS("/researchers/caitlin.page/cf_nano/r_output/optiles_all.rds")
dtu.optiles <- readRDS("/researchers/caitlin.page/cf_nano/r_output/ts.gene_optiles.rds")
dmrcate_seq_dmr <- readRDS("/researchers/caitlin.page/cf_nano/r_output/dmr_encode_gm12878_k562.rds")
all_samples_simp <- all_samples %>% distinct(seqnames, read_start, read_end, strand, sample, read_id, alpha, meth_pattern, num_meth, total)
colnames(all_samples_simp)[2:3] <- c("start", "end")
dtu_tiles_5_exon <- readRDS("/researchers/caitlin.page/cf_nano/r_output/dtu_tiles_5_exon.rds")
bin_delta <- find_overlaps(as_granges(all_samples_simp), as_granges(optiles_all)) %>% data.frame() %>%
  distinct(sample, read_id, start, end, alpha, region_id) %>% 
    mutate(alpha_group = case_when(alpha < 0.2 ~ "a < 0.2",
                                alpha > 0.8 ~ "a > 0.8",
                                alpha >= 0.2 & alpha <= 0.4 ~ "0.2 <= a <= 0.4",
                                alpha > 0.4 & alpha < 0.6 ~ "0.4 < a < 0.6",
                                TRUE ~ "0.6 <= a <= 0.8")) %>%
  mutate(transcript = paste0(region_id, "_", alpha_group)) %>% mutate(sample_type = ifelse(sample %in% c("b1", "b2"), "B", "CML")) %>%
  group_by(region_id, sample_type) %>% mutate(mean_alpha = mean(alpha)) %>% ungroup() %>% distinct(region_id, sample_type, mean_alpha) %>% .[order(.$region_id),]

bin_delta <- bin_delta %>% pivot_wider(names_from = sample_type, values_from = mean_alpha) %>% mutate(delta_b_minus_cml = B - CML)
bin_delta <- data.frame(bin_delta)

Analysis

overlap2 <- find_overlaps(as_granges(filter(dtu_tiles_5_exon, FDR < 0.05)), as_granges(dmrcate_seq_dmr)) %>% data.frame()
dtu_tiles_5_exon %>% filter(FDR < 0.05) %>% mutate(overlap_dmr = ifelse(region_id %in% overlap2$region_id, TRUE, FALSE)) %>%
  ggplot(aes(x = overlap_dmr, fill = transcript)) +
  geom_bar()

dtu_tiles_5_exon %>% filter(FDR < 0.05) %>% mutate(overlap_dmr = ifelse(region_id %in% overlap2$region_id, TRUE, FALSE)) %>%
  ggplot(aes(x = overlap_dmr, fill = transcript)) +
  geom_bar(position = "fill")

dtu_tiles_5_exon %>% filter(FDR < 0.05) %>% mutate(overlap_dmr = ifelse(region_id %in% overlap2$region_id, TRUE, FALSE)) %>%
  ggplot(aes(x = transcript, fill = overlap_dmr)) +
  geom_bar()

dtu_tiles_5_exon %>% filter(FDR < 0.05) %>% mutate(overlap_dmr = ifelse(region_id %in% overlap2$region_id, TRUE, FALSE)) %>%
  ggplot(aes(x = transcript, fill = overlap_dmr)) +
  geom_bar(position = "fill")

  filter(transcript == "0.4 < a < 0.6", overlap_dmr == FALSE)

optiles_all_beta %>% mutate(mid_not_sig_in_dmr = ifelse(region_id %in% interest, TRUE, FALSE)) %>%
  filter(!is.na(mean_b), !is.na(mean_cml)) %>%
  mutate(beta_group_b = case_when(mean_b > 0.4 & mean_b < 0.6 ~ "mid:0.4-0.6", 
                                mean_b < 0.2 ~ "low:<0.2",
                                mean_b > 0.8 ~ "high:>0.8",
                                mean_b >= 0.2 & mean_b <= 0.4 ~ "low-med:0.2-0.4",
                                TRUE ~ "med-high:0.6-0.8")) %>%
  mutate(beta_group_cml = case_when(mean_cml > 0.4 & mean_cml < 0.6 ~ "mid:0.4-0.6", 
                                mean_cml < 0.2 ~ "low:<0.2",
                                mean_cml > 0.8 ~ "high:>0.8",
                                mean_cml >= 0.2 & mean_cml <= 0.4 ~ "low-med:0.2-0.4",
                                TRUE ~ "med-high:0.6-0.8")) %>%
  ggplot(aes(x = beta_group_b, y = beta_group_cml, colour = mid_not_sig_in_dmr)) +
  geom_count()

  geom_bar(position = "fill")

mutate(alpha_group = case_when(alpha < 0.2 ~ “a < 0.2”, alpha > 0.8 ~ “a > 0.8”, alpha >= 0.2 & alpha <= 0.4 ~ “0.2 <= a <= 0.4”, alpha > 0.4 & alpha < 0.6 ~ “0.4 < a < 0.6”, TRUE ~ “0.6 <= a <= 0.8”))

filter(!is.na(mean_b), !is.na(mean_cml)) %>% mutate(mid_beta = ifelse(mean_b >= 0.4 & mean_b <= 0.6 | mean_cml >= 0.4 & mean_cml <= 0.6, TRUE, FALSE)) %>% group_by(region_id) %>% mutate(has_mid_beta = any(mid_beta == TRUE)) %>% ungroup() %>% distinct(region_id, sig_dmr, sig_dtu, has_mid_beta) %>% mutate(sig_dmr = ifelse(sig_dmr == TRUE, “dmr_sig”, “dmr_not_sig”), sig_dtu = ifelse(sig_dtu == TRUE, “dtu_sig”, “dtu_not_sig”)) %>% pivot_longer(cols = c(sig_dmr, sig_dtu), names_to = “sig”, values_to = “is_sig”) %>% .[,c(1,2,4)] %>% distinct() %>% ggplot(aes(x = is_sig, fill = has_mid_beta)) + geom_bar(position = “fill”)
